select * from emp, dept; 
select * from emp cross join dept; 


select * from customers, salespeople where customers.SNUM = salespeople.SNUM;

select * from customers join salespeople on customers.SNUM = salespeople.SNUM;

select * from customers inner join salespeople using(SNUM);


select customers.cname, salespeople.sname, orders.*  from customers join salespeople on customers.SNUM = salespeople.SNUM inner join orders on customers.cnum = orders.cnum;
